 ) a report has come out about how discrimination against Dalits and Muslims is done in renting or selling houses in urban areas of delhi-ncr
 EPW (economic and political vikali) dwaara kiye gaye is research ke nattejey chaunkaane vaale hai
 The research was carried out by a team of Professor SK Throat (chairman Indian Council of Social Science Research), Anuradha Banerjee and Vinod Mishra
 research ke dauraan phone par kiraye par makaan dilaane vaale tamaam agenton se baat kii gai
 Homes were found in the name of 1,479 people
 inamen oonchi jatiyon ke hindu naam,dalit or muslimonke naam shaamil the
 Surprisingly, agents received positive responses in the name of 493 upper caste Hindus, while agents refused to provide houses to about 18 per cent Dalits and 31 per cent Muslims
 is research main 198 logon ko sidhe agenton ke paas le jaaya gaya
 Among them, all but 66 upper caste Hindus were Dalits and Muslims
 lagbhag 97 fisadisavarna hinduonke maamle main agenton ne sakaaratmak jawaab die jabaki 44 fisadi daliton or 61 fisadi muslimon ke maamle main agenton ne makaan dene se saaf inkaar kar diya
 In the case of Dalits, about 51 per cent were willing to give agents a house with conditions while among Muslims it was up to 71 per cent
 throt ne kaha, 'yah saaf taur par bazaar kii asafalataa ko dikhaata he jahaan ek sampann dalit-muslim bhi achche ilaakon main ghar paane main mushkilon kaa saamana kar rahaa he
 This research also shows that the condition of Muslims in getting homes in delhi-ncr is worse than the Dalits
 ' pravaasiyon ke liye behatar jagah maane jane vaale dilli-ensiaar main lagbhag 18 fisadi daliton ko savarna makanamalikon dwaara saaf taur par makaan dene se inkaar kar diya gaya
 In the case of Dalits, about 23 per cent were willing to give them houses on rent but with many conditions which included higher rent and prohibition of many things

 is dauraan unhone 79 gendon kaa saamana kiya or paanch chauke lagaae
 He was lbw to Rahul Sharma
 jayavardhane kii jagah lene aae maithyuj ne sangakaara kaa acha saath nibhaayaa
 The two shared a 41-run partnership for the fifth wicket
 182 ke kul yoga par sangakaara bhi chalate bane
 He faced 95 balls and scored 73 runs
 is dauraan unhone paanch chauke lagaae
 By that time it seemed that the Sri Lankan team would not be able to cross the 250 mark, but Mathews, along with Mendis, not only pushed the innings forward but after that, without losing any wickets, the team's score reached 286
 maithyuj ne 57 gendon par 71 ranon kii tej pari kheli
 During this, he hit five fours and a six
 mendis ne 40 gendon par 45 ran banaae or teen chauke va ek chakka lagaaya
 Both shared an unbeaten 104-run partnership for the sixth wicket
 bharat kii ore se jahir khan sabase safal gendbaaj rahe
 He took two wickets
 pathan, ashok dinda or sharma ke khate main ek-ek wicket gaya
 Dinda proved to be very expensive
 apane 10 over ke cote main unhone 76 ran lutaae
 The comments shrunkhlaa main ab bhartiya team ne 2-1 kii badhat hasil kar lee he
 a change was made to the Sri Lankan team for this match
 ballebaaj lahiru thirimanne kii jagah jivan mendis ko srilanka kii antim ekadash team main jagah mili
 The Indian team made two changes in their team for this match
 leg spinner rahul sharma or tej gendbaaj ashok dinda ko pragyan ojha or umesh yadav kii jagah antim ekadash team main jagah mili
 The Indian team achieved the target of 287 runs laid by Sri Lanka by losing five wickets with two balls remaining
 bharat kii jeet main salaami ballebaaj gautam gambheer or madhyakram ke ballebaaj suresh raina or harfanmaulaa irfan pathan kii pramukh bhoomika rahi
 While Gambhir played a century of 102 runs, Raina scored 65 not out and Pathan scored 34 not out
 gambheer ne bhale hi shatkeey pari kheli lekin raina ne vipareet paristhiyon main yah match bharat kii jholii main daalkar apni pratibha kaa ek or parichay diya
 He was awarded the Man of the Match award for this outstanding performance
 lakshya kaa peechha karne utari bhartiya team ko duusare hi over main karaara jhatka laga jab visphotak salaami ballebaaj virendra sahvaag saste main apana wicket ganvaa baithe

 sahvaag sirf chah gendon kaa saamana kar sake

 thisara perera kii gend par sthanapann kshetrarakshak senanayake ne unka kaich lapka

 Kohli scored 38 runs
 unhone 65 gendon kaa saamana kiya or do chauke lagaae
 Rangana Herath caught his brilliant catch on his own ball
 iske baad captain mahendra singh dhoni ne khud maidan par morcha sambhaala
 He, along with Gambhir, moved the innings slowly forward
 lekin 36wein over kii pehali gend par dhoni bhi apana wicket ganvaa baithe
 He scored 31 runs, facing 60 balls
 lasith malinga ne unhen clin bold kar pavilion kii raah dikhaai
 Rohit Sharma who came to replace Dhoni proved to be a flop once again
 malinga kii pehali hi gend par vah chakma kha gaye or pagabaadha qaraar die gaye
 He could not even open his account
 malinga ne lagaataar do gendon par do wicket lekar bhartiya team ko ek baar phir baikfoot par dhakel diya

 vah ran out hue

 unhone 10 chauke lagaae

 lekin suresh raina or irfan pathan ne apane dam par is lakshya ko hasil kiya or bhartiya team ko jeet dilaai
 Raina scored 65 runs off 45 balls with the help of six fours and a six while Pathan scored 34 off 31 balls
 donon ke bich paanchaven wicket par 11

 isse pehle srilanka ne toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karte hue nirdhaarit 50 overon main chah wicket ke nuksaan par 286 ran banaae
 Sri Lanka's innings faltered after the initial setbacks
 usne mahaj 20 ke yoga par chotii ke teen ballebaajon ke wicket ganvaa die the lekin iske baad mahela jayavardhane or kumaar sangakaara ne milakar srilankai team ko mushkilon se nikaala
 Angelo Mathews and Jeevan Mendis scored a century partnership in the final overs to bring the team to a strong position
 srilanka ne toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji kaa faisla kiya tha
 Only nine runs were added to the total that Tilakaratne Dilshan was bowled by Zaheer Khan on a personal total of four runs and sent to the pavilion
 paanchaven over main 19 ke kul yoga par upul tharanga bhi chal die
 He could only score eight runs
 jahir kii gend par captain mahendra singh dhoni ne wicket ke peeche unka kaich lapka

 irfan pathan ne unhen pagabaadha out kiya
 After this, Sangakkara and Jayawardene shared 121 runs for the fourth wicket to take their team out of difficult situations

 gambheer ne jahaan 102 ranon kii shatkeey pari kheli vahiin raina ne naabad 65 or pathan ne naabad 34 ran banaae

 unhen is shandaar pradarshan ke liye main of da match kaa puraskaar diya gaya

 us samay bharat kaa score aath ran tha

 unhone teen ran banaae

 unhone 60 gendon kaa saamana karte hue 31 ran banaae

 vah apana khaataa bhi nahin khol sake

 vah aath ran hi bana sake

" kai vajahon masalan kisaanon ko adhik muaavje ke bhugtan tathaa utpaadan laagat main badhotaree se daam badhenge

 unhone kaha ki pichley dedh saal main nirmaan saamagree kii keemton tathaa byaaj daron main kaaphi ijapha hua he
